/app/api/auth/login/route.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
 2 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 3 | import bcrypt from 'bcrypt';
 4 | import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';
 5 | import { LoginWithTenantDto } from '@/lib/dto/tenant';
 6 | import { getTenantDb } from '@/lib/db';
 7 | import * as tenantSchema from '@/lib/db/schema/tenant';
 8 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
 9 | import log from '@/lib/logger';
10 | 
11 | export const runtime = 'nodejs';
12 | 
13 | export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
14 |   try {
15 |     const body = await request.json();
16 |     const { tenantId, email, password } = LoginWithTenantDto.parse(body);
17 | 
18 |     log.info({ tenantId, email }, '[API] Login attempt.');
19 | 
20 |     const tenantDb = await getTenantDb(tenantId);
21 |     const userResult = await tenantDb.query.users.findFirst({
22 |       where: eq(tenantSchema.users.email, email),
23 |     });
24 | 
25 |     if (!userResult) {
26 |       log.warn({ tenantId, email }, '[API] Login failed: User not found.');
27 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' }, { status: 401 });
28 |     }
29 | 
30 |     const isPasswordValid = await bcrypt.compare(password, userResult.password);
31 |     if (!isPasswordValid) {
32 |       log.warn({ tenantId, email }, '[API] Login failed: Invalid password.');
33 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' }, { status: 401 });
34 |     }
35 | 
36 |     const token = jwt.sign({ tenantId, userId: userResult.id }, env.JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn: '8h' });
37 |     log.info({ tenantId, userId: userResult.id }, '[API] Login successful.');
38 | 
39 |     const response = NextResponse.json({ message: 'Login successful' });
40 |     response.cookies.set('authToken', token, {
41 |       httpOnly: true,
42 |       secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production',
43 |       sameSite: 'strict',
44 |       path: '/',
45 |       maxAge: 8 * 60 * 60, // 8 hours
46 |     });
47 | 
48 |     return response;
49 | 
50 |   } catch (err) {
51 |     log.error({ error: err }, '[API] Login process failed.');
52 |     if (err instanceof Error && err.message === 'Tenant not found') {
53 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid tenant specified' }, { status: 404 });
54 |     }
55 |     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'An internal error occurred' }, { status: 500 });
56 |   }
57 | }


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/app/api/tenants/route.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // In /app/api/tenants/route.ts
 2 | 
 3 | import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
 4 | import { z } from 'zod';
 5 | import bcrypt from 'bcrypt';
 6 | import { TenantSignupDto } from '@/lib/dto/tenant';
 7 | import { createNeonProject } from '@/lib/neon/api';
 8 | import { mainDb, getTenantDb } from '@/lib/db';
 9 | import { tenants } from '@/lib/db/schema/shared';
10 | import * as tenantSchema from '@/lib/db/schema/tenant';
11 | import { encrypt } from '@/lib/crypto';
12 | import { runTenantMigrations } from '@/lib/db/migrate';
13 | import log from '@/lib/logger';
14 | 
15 | export const runtime = 'nodejs';
16 | 
17 | export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
18 |   let neonProjectId: string | null = null;
19 |   try {
20 | const body = await request.json();
21 |     const data = TenantSignupDto.parse(body);
22 |     const { tenantId, orgName, adminName, adminEmail, adminPassword } = data;
23 | 
24 |     log.info({ tenantId }, '[API] Tenant creation request received.');
25 | 
26 |     // 1. Create the new database project on Neon
27 |     const neonProject = await createNeonProject(tenantId);
28 |     if (!neonProject || !neonProject.projectId || !neonProject.connectionString) {
29 |       throw new Error("Invalid response from Neon API during project creation.");
30 |     }
31 |     const { projectId: _neonProjectId, connectionString } = neonProject;
32 |     neonProjectId = _neonProjectId; // Assign to the outer scope variable for the catch block
33 | 
34 |     // 2. Store the new tenant's metadata in your main database
35 |     const encryptedConnectionString = encrypt(connectionString);
36 |     await mainDb.insert(tenants).values({
37 |       tenantId,
38 |       name: orgName,
39 |       neonProjectId: _neonProjectId, // Use the non-nullable constant here
40 |       connectionString: encryptedConnectionString,
41 |     });
42 |     log.info({ tenantId, neonProjectId }, '[API] Tenant metadata stored.');
43 | 
44 |     // 3. Run the migrations on the newly created tenant database
45 |     await runTenantMigrations(connectionString);
46 | 
47 |     // 4. Create the tenant's first admin user in their new database
48 |     const tenantDb = await getTenantDb(tenantId);
49 |     const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(adminPassword, 12);
50 |     await tenantDb.insert(tenantSchema.users).values({
51 |       name: adminName,
52 |       email: adminEmail,
53 |       password: hashedPassword,
54 |     });
55 |     log.info({ tenantId, adminEmail }, '[API] Admin user created in tenant DB.');
56 | 
57 |     // 5. Done!
58 |     return NextResponse.json({ message: 'Tenant created successfully', tenantId });
59 | 
60 |   } catch (err) {
61 |     // --- THIS IS THE NEW, IMPROVED CATCH BLOCK ---
62 |     let errorDetails = {};
63 |     if (err instanceof Error) {
64 |         errorDetails = {
65 |             name: err.name,
66 |             message: err.message,
67 |             stack: err.stack,
68 |         };
69 |     } else {
70 |         errorDetails = { error: 'An unknown error occurred' };
71 |     }
72 |     
73 |     log.error({ ...errorDetails, neonProjectId }, '[API] Tenant creation failed.');
74 |     // --- END OF NEW CATCH BLOCK ---
75 | 
76 |     if (err instanceof z.ZodError) {
77 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid input', details: err }, { status: 400 });
78 |     }
79 |     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal server error' }, { status: 500 });
80 |   }
81 | }

/app/dashboard/page.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | import { cookies } from 'next/headers';
 2 | import { verify } from 'jsonwebtoken';
 3 | import { getTenantDb } from '@/lib/db';
 4 | import * as tenantSchema from '@/lib/db/schema/tenant';
 5 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 6 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
 7 | import { redirect } from 'next/navigation';
 8 | import log from '@/lib/logger';
 9 | 
10 | export const dynamic = 'force-dynamic';
11 | 
12 | interface UserSession {
13 |   tenantId: string;
14 |   userId: number;
15 | }
16 | 
17 | export default async function DashboardPage() {
18 |   const cookieStore = await cookies();
19 |   const token = cookieStore.get('authToken')?.value;
20 | 
21 |   if (!token) {
22 |     log.warn(' No auth token found, redirecting to login.');
23 |     redirect('/login');
24 |   }
25 | 
26 |   try {
27 |     const decoded = verify(token, env.JWT_SECRET) as UserSession;
28 |     log.info({ session: decoded }, ' User session decoded.');
29 | 
30 |     const tenantDb = await getTenantDb(decoded.tenantId);
31 |     const userResult = await tenantDb.query.users.findFirst({
32 |       where: eq(tenantSchema.users.id, decoded.userId),
33 |     });
34 | 
35 |     if (!userResult) {
36 |       log.error({ session: decoded }, ' User not found in tenant DB.');
37 |       cookieStore.delete('authToken');
38 |       redirect('/login');
39 |     }
40 | 
41 |     return (
42 |       <div className="min-h-screen p-8 bg-gray-100 text-gray-900">
43 |         <h1 className="text-4xl font-bold">Welcome to Tenant: <span className="text-blue-600">{decoded.tenantId}</span> Dashboard</h1>
44 |         <p className="text-xl mt-4">Logged in as: {userResult.name}</p>
45 |         <p className="text-xl mt-4">User email in as: {userResult.email}</p>
46 |         
47 |       </div>
48 |     );
49 |   } catch (err) {
50 |     log.error({ error: err }, ' Authorization failed.');
51 |     cookieStore.delete('authToken');
52 |     redirect('/login');
53 |   }
54 | }

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/app/login/page.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // app/login/page.tsx
 2 | 'use client';
 3 | 
 4 | import { useState } from 'react';
 5 | import { useForm } from 'react-hook-form';
 6 | import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
 7 | import { LoginWithTenantInput, LoginWithTenantDto } from '@/lib/dto/tenant';
 8 | 
 9 | export default function LoginPage() {
10 |   const [message, setMessage] = useState('');
11 |   const { register, handleSubmit, formState: { errors } } = useForm<LoginWithTenantInput>({
12 |     resolver: zodResolver(LoginWithTenantDto),
13 |   });
14 | 
15 |   const onSubmit = async (data: LoginWithTenantInput) => {
16 |     setMessage('');
17 |     try {
18 |       const res = await fetch('/api/auth/login', {
19 |         method: 'POST',
20 |         headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
21 |         body: JSON.stringify(data),
22 |       });
23 | 
24 |       if (res.ok) {
25 |         setMessage('Login successful! Redirecting...');
26 |         window.location.href = `http://${data.tenantId}.localhost:3000/dashboard`;
27 |       } else {
28 |         const result = await res.json();
29 |         setMessage(result.error || 'Login failed');
30 |       }
31 |     } catch (error) {
32 |       setMessage('An unexpected error occurred.');
33 |       console.error('Login request failed:', error);
34 |     }
35 |   };
36 | 
37 |   return (
38 |     <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gray-900 text-white">
39 |       <form onSubmit={handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="bg-gray-800 p-8 rounded-lg shadow-xl w-full max-w-md">
40 |         <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-6 text-center">Login to Your School</h1>
41 |         <div className="mb-4">
42 |           <input {...register('tenantId')} placeholder="School ID (e.g., frisco-high)" className="p-3 bg-gray-700 border border-gray-600 w-full rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500" />
43 |           {errors.tenantId && <p className="text-red-500 text-sm mt-1">{errors.tenantId.message}</p>}
44 |         </div>
45 |         <div className="mb-4">
46 |           <input {...register('email')} placeholder="Email" className="p-3 bg-gray-700 border border-gray-600 w-full rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500" />
47 |           {errors.email && <p className="text-red-500 text-sm mt-1">{errors.email.message}</p>}
48 |         </div>
49 |         <div className="mb-6">
50 |           <input type="password" {...register('password')} placeholder="Password" className="p-3 bg-gray-700 border border-gray-600 w-full rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500" />
51 |           {errors.password && <p className="text-red-500 text-sm mt-1">{errors.password.message}</p>}
52 |         </div>
53 |         <button type="submit" className="bg-blue-600 text-white p-3 w-full rounded-md hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors">Login</button>
54 |         {message && <p className="mt-4 text-center text-red-400">{message}</p>}
55 |       </form>
56 |     </div>
57 |   );
58 | }

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/app/signup/page.tsx:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // app/signup/page.tsx
 2 | 'use client';
 3 | import { useForm } from 'react-hook-form';
 4 | import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
 5 | import { TenantSignupInput, TenantSignupDto } from '@/lib/dto/tenant';
 6 | import { useState } from 'react';
 7 | import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
 8 | 
 9 | export default function SignupPage() {
10 |   const [message, setMessage] = useState('');
11 |   const router = useRouter();
12 |   const { register, handleSubmit, formState: { errors } } = useForm<TenantSignupInput>({
13 |     resolver: zodResolver(TenantSignupDto),
14 |   });
15 | 
16 |   const onSubmit = async (data: TenantSignupInput) => {
17 |     const res = await fetch('/api/tenants', {
18 |       method: 'POST',
19 |       headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
20 |       body: JSON.stringify(data),
21 |     });
22 |     const result = await res.json();
23 |     if (res.ok) {
24 |       setMessage(`Tenant created! Redirecting to dashboard...`);
25 |       // Redirect to tenant dashboard (add to /etc/hosts first)
26 |       window.location.href = `http://${data.tenantId}.localhost:3000/dashboard`;
27 |     } else {
28 |       setMessage(result.error || 'Error creating tenant');
29 |     }
30 |   };
31 | 
32 |   return (
33 |     <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gray-800">
34 |       <form onSubmit={handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="bg-white p-8 rounded shadow-md w-96">
35 |         <h1 className="text-2xl mb-4">Tenant Signup</h1>
36 |         <input {...register('orgName')} placeholder="Organization Name" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
37 |         {errors.orgName && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.orgName.message}</p>}
38 |         <input {...register('tenantId')} placeholder="Tenant ID (e.g., plano-isd)" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
39 |         {errors.tenantId && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.tenantId.message}</p>}
40 |         <input {...register('adminName')} placeholder="Admin Name" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
41 |         {errors.adminName && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.adminName.message}</p>}
42 |         <input {...register('adminEmail')} placeholder="Admin Email" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
43 |         {errors.adminEmail && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.adminEmail.message}</p>}
44 |         <input type="password" {...register('adminPassword')} placeholder="Admin Password" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
45 |         {errors.adminPassword && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.adminPassword.message}</p>}
46 |         <button type="submit" className="bg-blue-500 text-white p-2 w-full">Signup</button>
47 |         <p className="mt-2 text-center">{message}</p>
48 |       </form>
49 |     </div>
50 |   );
51 | }

/lib/crypto.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | import { createCipheriv, createDecipheriv, scryptSync, randomBytes } from 'crypto';
 2 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
 3 | 
 4 | const ALGORITHM = 'aes-256-gcm';
 5 | const IV_LENGTH = 16;
 6 | const TAG_LENGTH = 16;
 7 | const KEY = scryptSync(env.ENCRYPTION_KEY, 'salt', 32);
 8 | 
 9 | export function encrypt(text: string): string {
10 |   const iv = randomBytes(IV_LENGTH);
11 |   const cipher = createCipheriv(ALGORITHM, KEY, iv);
12 |   const encrypted = Buffer.concat([cipher.update(text, 'utf8'), cipher.final()]);
13 |   const tag = cipher.getAuthTag();
14 |   return Buffer.concat([iv, tag, encrypted]).toString('hex');
15 | }
16 | 
17 | export function decrypt(encryptedText: string): string {
18 |   const data = Buffer.from(encryptedText, 'hex');
19 |   const iv = data.slice(0, IV_LENGTH);
20 |   const tag = data.slice(IV_LENGTH, IV_LENGTH + TAG_LENGTH);
21 |   const encrypted = data.slice(IV_LENGTH + TAG_LENGTH);
22 |   const decipher = createDecipheriv(ALGORITHM, KEY, iv);
23 |   decipher.setAuthTag(tag);
24 |   const decrypted = Buffer.concat([decipher.update(encrypted), decipher.final()]);
25 |   return decrypted.toString('utf8');
26 | }


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/lib/db/index.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // lib/db/index.ts
 2 | import { drizzle, NodePgDatabase } from 'drizzle-orm/node-postgres';
 3 | import { Pool } from 'pg';
 4 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 5 | import { tenants } from './schema/shared';
 6 | import * as tenantSchema from './schema/tenant';
 7 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
 8 | import { decrypt } from '@/lib/crypto';
 9 | import log from '@/lib/logger';
10 | 
11 | // 1. Main DB Client (for managing tenant metadata)
12 | const mainPool = new Pool({ connectionString: env.POSTGRES_URL });
13 | export const mainDb = drizzle(mainPool, { schema: { tenants } });
14 | 
15 | // 2. Tenant DB Client Cache
16 | const tenantDbCache = new Map<string, NodePgDatabase<typeof tenantSchema>>();
17 | 
18 | // 3. Function to get a tenant-specific DB client
19 | export async function getTenantDb(tenantId: string): Promise<NodePgDatabase<typeof tenantSchema>> {
20 |   if (tenantDbCache.has(tenantId)) {
21 |     log.info({ tenantId }, 'Tenant DB client cache HIT.');
22 |     return tenantDbCache.get(tenantId)!;
23 |   }
24 |   log.info({ tenantId }, 'Tenant DB client cache MISS.');
25 | 
26 |   const results = await mainDb
27 |     .select({ connectionString: tenants.connectionString })
28 |     .from(tenants)
29 |     .where(eq(tenants.tenantId, tenantId))
30 |     .limit(1);
31 | 
32 |   // --- Start of Fix ---
33 |   const tenantData = results[0]; // Access the first element of the array
34 | 
35 |   if (!tenantData) {
36 |     log.error({ tenantId }, 'Tenant not found in main database.');
37 |     throw new Error('Tenant not found');
38 |   }
39 | 
40 |   const decryptedConnectionString = decrypt(tenantData.connectionString);
41 |   // --- End of Fix ---
42 | 
43 |   const tenantPool = new Pool({ connectionString: decryptedConnectionString });
44 |   const tenantDb = drizzle(tenantPool, { schema: tenantSchema });
45 | 
46 |   tenantDbCache.set(tenantId, tenantDb);
47 |   log.info({ tenantId }, 'Created and cached new tenant DB client.');
48 | 
49 |   return tenantDb;
50 | }


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/lib/db/migrate.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // In /lib/db/migrate.ts
 2 | import { drizzle } from 'drizzle-orm/postgres-js';
 3 | import { migrate } from 'drizzle-orm/postgres-js/migrator';
 4 | import postgres from 'postgres';
 5 | import log from '@/lib/logger';
 6 | 
 7 | export async function runTenantMigrations(connectionString: string) {
 8 |   // Use postgres 'on-the-fly' with max 1 connection for migrations
 9 |   const migrationClient = postgres(connectionString, { max: 1 });
10 |   const db = drizzle(migrationClient);
11 | 
12 |   try {
13 |     log.info('Starting tenant migration...');
14 |     await migrate(db, { migrationsFolder: './drizzle/tenant' }); // Assumes tenant migrations are in 'drizzle/tenant'
15 |     log.info('Tenant migration completed successfully.');
16 |   } catch (error) {
17 |     log.error({ error }, 'Tenant migration failed.');
18 |     // Re-throw the error to ensure the API call fails loudly
19 |     throw new Error('Could not run tenant migrations.');
20 |   } finally {
21 |     // Ensure the connection is closed
22 |     await migrationClient.end();
23 |   }
24 | }

/lib/neon/api.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // In lib/neon/api.ts
 2 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
 3 | import log from '@/lib/logger';
 4 | 
 5 | const NEON_API_BASE = 'https://console.neon.tech/api/v2';
 6 | 
 7 | export async function createNeonProject(tenantId: string) {
 8 |   log.info({ tenantId }, '[NeonAPI] Starting project creation process.');
 9 | 
10 |   const headers = {
11 |     'Authorization': `Bearer ${env.NEON_API_KEY}`,
12 |     'Content-Type': 'application/json',
13 |     'Accept': 'application/json',
14 |   };
15 | 
16 |   const projectResponse = await fetch(`${NEON_API_BASE}/projects`, {
17 |     method: 'POST',
18 |     headers,
19 |     body: JSON.stringify({
20 |       project: { name: `edux-tenant-${tenantId}` },
21 |     }),
22 |   });
23 | 
24 |   if (!projectResponse.ok) {
25 |     const errorBody = await projectResponse.text();
26 |     log.error({ tenantId, status: projectResponse.status, errorBody }, '[NeonAPI] Failed to create project.');
27 |     throw new Error(`Failed to create Neon project: ${errorBody}`);
28 |   }
29 | 
30 |   const responseData = await projectResponse.json();
31 |   const project = responseData.project;
32 |   const connectionDetails = responseData.connection_uris?.[0];
33 |   const connection_uri = connectionDetails?.connection_uri;
34 | 
35 |   if (!connection_uri) {
36 |     log.error({ responseData }, '[NeonAPI] Connection URI could not be extracted from the response.');
37 |     throw new Error('Connection URI could not be extracted from the Neon API response.');
38 |   }
39 | 
40 |   log.info({ tenantId, projectId: project.id }, '[NeonAPI] Project created successfully.');
41 | 
42 |   // The modification to create a pooled string has been removed.
43 |   // We will now return the original, direct connection string.
44 | 
45 |   return {
46 |     projectId: project.id,
47 |     connectionString: connection_uri,
48 |   };
49 | }

/lib/server/tenant.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // lib/server/tenant.ts
 2 | import { mainDb } from '@/lib/db';
 3 | import { tenants } from '@/lib/db/schema/shared';
 4 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 5 | 
 6 | export async function validateTenant(tenantId: string) {
 7 |   console.log(`[Tenant] Validating tenant: ${tenantId}`);
 8 |   const results = await mainDb.select().from(tenants).where(eq(tenants.tenantId, tenantId)).limit(1);
 9 |   const tenant = results[0];
10 | 
11 |   if (!tenant) {
12 |     console.error(`[Tenant] Invalid tenant: ${tenantId}`);
13 |     throw new Error('Tenant not found');
14 |   }
15 | 
16 |   return tenant;
17 | }

/middleware.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // middleware.ts
 2 | import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
 3 | import logger from './lib/logger';
 4 | 
 5 | // Extracts the tenant ID from the hostname.
 6 | const getTenantId = (host: string): string | null => {
 7 |   const parts = host.split('.');
 8 | 
 9 |   // Handles tenant.localhost:3000 in development
10 |   if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' && parts.length === 2 && parts[1].startsWith('localhost')) {
11 |     return parts[0];
12 |   }
13 | 
14 |   // Handles tenant.example.com in production
15 |   if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' && parts.length > 1 && parts[0] !== 'www') {
16 |     return parts[0];
17 |   }
18 | 
19 |   return null;
20 | };
21 | 
22 | 
23 | export function middleware(request: NextRequest) {
24 |   const host = request.headers.get('host') || '';
25 |   const tenantId = getTenantId(host);
26 |   const { pathname } = request.nextUrl;
27 |   const log = logger.child({ tenantId, pathname });
28 | 
29 |   log.info('Middleware processing request');
30 | 
31 |   const headers = new Headers(request.headers);
32 |   if (tenantId) {
33 |     headers.set('x-tenant-id', tenantId);
34 |   }
35 | 
36 |   // Allow public routes regardless of tenant.
37 |   if (pathname === '/' || pathname === '/signup') {
38 |     return NextResponse.next({ request: { headers } });
39 |   }
40 | 
41 |   // If on a tenant subdomain, allow access to login.
42 |   if (tenantId && pathname.startsWith('/login')) {
43 |       return NextResponse.next({ request: { headers } });
44 |   }
45 | 
46 |   // All API routes are allowed to pass through for now;
47 |   // authentication will be handled at the route level.
48 |   if (pathname.startsWith('/api')) {
49 |     return NextResponse.next({ request: { headers } });
50 |   }
51 | 
52 |   // For dashboard access, check for an auth token.
53 |   const token = request.cookies.get('authToken');
54 |   if (pathname.startsWith('/dashboard') && !token) {
55 |     log.warn('Access to dashboard denied without token, redirecting to login.');
56 |     const loginUrl = new URL('/login', request.url);
57 |     return NextResponse.redirect(loginUrl);
58 |   }
59 | 
60 |   return NextResponse.next({ request: { headers } });
61 | }
62 | 
63 | export const config = {
64 |   matcher: [
65 |     /*
66 |      * Match all request paths except for the ones starting with:
67 |      * - _next/static (static files)
68 |      * - _next/image (image optimization files)
69 |      * - favicon.ico (favicon file)
70 |      */
71 |     '/((?!_next/static|_next/image|favicon.ico).*)',
72 |   ],
73 | };

6 |

 109 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 110 | /app/api/auth/login/route.ts:
 111 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 112 |  1 | // app/api/auth/login/route.ts
 113 |  2 | import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
 114 |  3 | import { getTenantDb } from '@/lib/db';
 115 |  4 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 116 |  5 | import bcrypt from 'bcrypt';
 117 |  6 | import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';
 118 |  7 | import { LoginDto } from '@/lib/dto/tenant';
 119 |  8 | import { validateTenant } from '@/lib/server/tenant';
 120 |  9 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
 121 | 10 | 
 122 | 11 | export const runtime = 'nodejs';
 123 | 12 | 
 124 | 13 | export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
 125 | 14 |   try {
 126 | 15 |     const tenantId = request.headers.get('x-tenant-id');
 127 | 16 |     if (!tenantId) {
 128 | 17 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Tenant required' }, { status: 400 });
 129 | 18 |     }
 130 | 19 | 
 131 | 20 |     // Validate tenant existence
 132 | 21 |     await validateTenant(tenantId);
 133 | 22 | 
 134 | 23 |     const body = await request.json();
 135 | 24 |     const data = LoginDto.parse(body);
 136 | 25 | 
 137 | 26 |     console.log(`[API] Login attempt for tenant: ${tenantId}, email: ${data.email}`);
 138 | 27 | 
 139 | 28 |     const { db: tenantDb, schema } = await getTenantDb(tenantId);
 140 | 29 |     const users = await tenantDb.select().from(schema.users).where(eq(schema.users.email, data.email)).limit(1);
 141 | 30 | 
 142 | 31 |     if (!users.length) {
 143 | 32 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' }, { status: 401 });
 144 | 33 |     }
 145 | 34 | 
 146 | 35 |     const user = users[0];
 147 | 36 |     const match = await bcrypt.compare(data.password, user.password);
 148 | 37 |     if (!match) {
 149 | 38 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' }, { status: 401 });
 150 | 39 |     }
 151 | 40 | 
 152 | 41 |     const token = jwt.sign({ tenantId, userId: user.id }, env.JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn: '1h' });
 153 | 42 | 
 154 | 43 |     const response = NextResponse.json({ message: 'Login successful' });
 155 | 44 |     response.cookies.set('authToken', token, { httpOnly: true, secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production', sameSite: 'strict', maxAge: 3600 });
 156 | 45 |     return response;
 157 | 46 |   } catch (err) {
 158 | 47 |     console.error('[API] Login failed:', err);
 159 | 48 |     if (err instanceof Error && err.message === 'Tenant not found') {
 160 | 49 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Tenant not found' }, { status: 404 });
 161 | 50 |     }
 162 | 51 |     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal error' }, { status: 500 });
 163 | 52 |   }
 164 | 53 | }
 165 | 
 166 | 
 167 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 168 | /app/api/tenants/route.ts:
 169 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 170 |  1 | // app/api/tenants/route.ts
 171 |  2 | import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
 172 |  3 | import { sharedDb, getTenantDb, executeRawQuery } from '@/lib/db';
 173 |  4 | import { tenants } from '@/lib/db/schema/shared';
 174 |  5 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 175 |  6 | import bcrypt from 'bcrypt';
 176 |  7 | import { TenantSignupDto } from '@/lib/dto/tenant';
 177 |  8 | import z from 'zod/v4';
 178 |  9 | 
 179 | 10 | export const runtime = 'nodejs';
 180 | 11 | 
 181 | 12 | export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
 182 | 13 |   try {
 183 | 14 |     const body = await request.json();
 184 | 15 |     const data = TenantSignupDto.parse(body);
 185 | 16 |     const tenantId = data.tenantId; 
 186 | 17 |     const schemaName = `tenant_${tenantId}`;
 187 | 18 | 
 188 | 19 |     console.log(`[API] Creating tenant: ${tenantId}, schema: ${schemaName}`);
 189 | 20 | 
 190 | 21 |     const existing = await sharedDb.select().from(tenants).where(eq(tenants.tenantId, tenantId));
 191 | 22 |     if (existing.length) {
 192 | 23 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Tenant ID already exists' }, { status: 409 });
 193 | 24 |     }
 194 | 25 | 
 195 | 26 |     // Create schema and users table
 196 | 27 |     await executeRawQuery(`CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS "${schemaName}";`);
 197 | 28 |     await executeRawQuery(`
 198 | 29 |       CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "${schemaName}".users (
 199 | 30 |         id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
 200 | 31 |         name TEXT NOT NULL,
 201 | 32 |         email TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
 202 | 33 |         password TEXT NOT NULL
 203 | 34 |       );
 204 | 35 |     `);
 205 | 36 | 
 206 | 37 |     // Insert tenant metadata
 207 | 38 |     await sharedDb.insert(tenants).values({
 208 | 39 |       tenantId,
 209 | 40 |       schemaName,
 210 | 41 |       name: data.orgName,
 211 | 42 |     });
 212 | 43 | 
 213 | 44 |     // Insert admin user
 214 | 45 |     const { db: tenantDb, schema } = await getTenantDb(tenantId);
 215 | 46 |     const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(data.adminPassword, 12);  // Stronger salt (12 rounds)
 216 | 47 |     await tenantDb.insert(schema.users).values({
 217 | 48 |       name: data.adminName,
 218 | 49 |       email: data.adminEmail,
 219 | 50 |       password: hashedPassword,
 220 | 51 |     });
 221 | 52 | 
 222 | 53 |     console.log(`[API] Tenant created successfully: ${tenantId}`);
 223 | 54 |     return NextResponse.json({ message: 'Tenant created', tenantId });
 224 | 55 |   } catch (err) {
 225 | 56 |     console.error('[API] Tenant creation failed:', err);
 226 | 57 |     if (err instanceof z.ZodError) {
 227 | 58 |       return NextResponse.json({ error: err }, { status: 400 });
 228 | 59 |     }
 229 | 60 |     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal error' }, { status: 500 });
 230 | 61 |   }
 231 | 62 | }

 234 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 235 | /app/dashboard/page.tsx:
 236 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 237 |  1 | // app/dashboard/page.tsx
 238 |  2 | import { cookies } from 'next/headers';
 239 |  3 | import { verify } from 'jsonwebtoken';
 240 |  4 | import { getTenantDb } from '@/lib/db';
 241 |  5 | 
 242 |  6 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 243 |  7 | import { env } from '@/env.mjs';
 244 |  8 | 
 245 |  9 | export const runtime = 'nodejs';  // Node runtime
 246 | 10 | 
 247 | 11 | export default async function DashboardPage() {
 248 | 12 |   const cookieStore = cookies();
 249 | 13 |   const token = (await cookieStore).get('authToken')?.value;
 250 | 14 |   if (!token) {
 251 | 15 |     return <div>Unauthorized</div>;
 252 | 16 |   }
 253 | 17 | 
 254 | 18 |   let decoded;
 255 | 19 |   try {
 256 | 20 |     decoded = verify(token, env.JWT_SECRET) as { tenantId: string; userId: number };
 257 | 21 | 
 258 | 22 |     const { db: tenantDb, schema } = await getTenantDb(decoded.tenantId);
 259 | 23 |     const user = await tenantDb.select().from(schema.users).where(eq(schema.users.id, decoded.userId)).limit(1);
 260 | 24 | 
 261 | 25 |     return (
 262 | 26 |       <div className="min-h-screen p-8 bg-gray-100">
 263 | 27 |         <h1 className="text-3xl">Welcome to {decoded.tenantId} Dashboard</h1>
 264 | 28 |         <p>Email: {user[0]?.email}</p>
 265 | 29 |       </div>
 266 | 30 |     );
 267 | 31 |   } catch (err) {
 268 | 32 |     if (err === 'Tenant not found') {
 269 | 33 |       return <div>Tenant not found</div>;
 270 | 34 |     }
 271 | 35 |     return <div>Invalid token</div>;
 272 | 36 |   }
 273 | 37 | }

 450 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 451 | /app/login/page.tsx:
 452 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 453 |  1 | // app/login/page.tsx
 454 |  2 | 'use client';
 455 |  3 | import { useForm } from 'react-hook-form';
 456 |  4 | import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
 457 |  5 | import { LoginInput, LoginDto } from '@/lib/dto/tenant';
 458 |  6 | import { useState } from 'react';
 459 |  7 | import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
 460 |  8 | 
 461 |  9 | export default function LoginPage() {
 462 | 10 |   const [message, setMessage] = useState('');
 463 | 11 |   const router = useRouter();
 464 | 12 |   const { register, handleSubmit, formState: { errors } } = useForm<LoginInput>({
 465 | 13 |     resolver: zodResolver(LoginDto),
 466 | 14 |   });
 467 | 15 | 
 468 | 16 |   const onSubmit = async (data: LoginInput) => {
 469 | 17 |     const res = await fetch('/api/auth/login', {
 470 | 18 |       method: 'POST',
 471 | 19 |       headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
 472 | 20 |       body: JSON.stringify(data),
 473 | 21 |     });
 474 | 22 |     if (res.ok) {
 475 | 23 |       router.push('/dashboard');
 476 | 24 |     } else {
 477 | 25 |       const result = await res.json();
 478 | 26 |       setMessage(result.error || 'Login failed');
 479 | 27 |     }
 480 | 28 |   };
 481 | 29 | 
 482 | 30 |   return (
 483 | 31 |     <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gray-800">
 484 | 32 |       <form onSubmit={handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="bg-green p-8 rounded shadow-md w-96">
 485 | 33 |         <h1 className="text-2xl mb-4">Login</h1>
 486 | 34 |         <input {...register('email')} placeholder="Email" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
 487 | 35 |         {errors.email && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.email.message}</p>}
 488 | 36 |         <input type="password" {...register('password')} placeholder="Password" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
 489 | 37 |         {errors.password && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.password.message}</p>}
 490 | 38 |         <button type="submit" className="bg-blue-500 text-white p-2 w-full">Login</button>
 491 | 39 |         <p className="mt-2">{message}</p>
 492 | 40 |       </form>
 493 | 41 |     </div>
 494 | 42 |   );
 495 | 43 | }

 499 | /app/page.tsx:
 500 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 501 |  1 | // app/page.tsx
 502 |  2 | import Link from 'next/link';
 503 |  3 | 
 504 |  4 | export default function HomePage() {

 525 |  1 | // app/signup/page.tsx
 526 |  2 | 'use client';
 527 |  3 | import { useForm } from 'react-hook-form';
 528 |  4 | import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
 529 |  5 | import { TenantSignupInput, TenantSignupDto } from '@/lib/dto/tenant';
 530 |  6 | import { useState } from 'react';
 531 |  7 | import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
 532 |  8 | 
 533 |  9 | export default function SignupPage() {
 534 | 10 |   const [message, setMessage] = useState('');
 535 | 11 |   const router = useRouter();
 536 | 12 |   const { register, handleSubmit, formState: { errors } } = useForm<TenantSignupInput>({
 537 | 13 |     resolver: zodResolver(TenantSignupDto),
 538 | 14 |   });
 539 | 15 | 
 540 | 16 |   const onSubmit = async (data: TenantSignupInput) => {
 541 | 17 |     const res = await fetch('/api/tenants', {
 542 | 18 |       method: 'POST',
 543 | 19 |       headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
 544 | 20 |       body: JSON.stringify(data),
 545 | 21 |     });
 546 | 22 |     const result = await res.json();
 547 | 23 |     if (res.ok) {
 548 | 24 |       setMessage(`Tenant created! Redirecting to dashboard...`);
 549 | 25 |       // Redirect to tenant dashboard (add to /etc/hosts first)
 550 | 26 |       window.location.href = `http://${data.tenantId}.localhost:3000/dashboard`;
 551 | 27 |     } else {
 552 | 28 |       setMessage(result.error || 'Error creating tenant');
 553 | 29 |     }
 554 | 30 |   };
 555 | 31 | 
 556 | 32 |   return (
 557 | 33 |     <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gray-800">
 558 | 34 |       <form onSubmit={handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="bg-white p-8 rounded shadow-md w-96">
 559 | 35 |         <h1 className="text-2xl mb-4">Tenant Signup</h1>
 560 | 36 |         <input {...register('orgName')} placeholder="Organization Name" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
 561 | 37 |         {errors.orgName && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.orgName.message}</p>}
 562 | 38 |         <input {...register('tenantId')} placeholder="Tenant ID (e.g., plano-isd)" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
 563 | 39 |         {errors.tenantId && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.tenantId.message}</p>}
 564 | 40 |         <input {...register('adminName')} placeholder="Admin Name" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
 565 | 41 |         {errors.adminName && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.adminName.message}</p>}
 566 | 42 |         <input {...register('adminEmail')} placeholder="Admin Email" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
 567 | 43 |         {errors.adminEmail && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.adminEmail.message}</p>}
 568 | 44 |         <input type="password" {...register('adminPassword')} placeholder="Admin Password" className="mb-2 p-2 border w-full" />
 569 | 45 |         {errors.adminPassword && <p className="text-red-500">{errors.adminPassword.message}</p>}
 570 | 46 |         <button type="submit" className="bg-blue-500 text-white p-2 w-full">Signup</button>
 571 | 47 |         <p className="mt-2 text-center">{message}</p>
 572 | 48 |       </form>
 573 | 49 |     </div>
 574 | 50 |   );

 920 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 921 | /lib/db/index.ts:
 922 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 923 |  1 | // lib/db/index.ts
 924 |  2 | import { drizzle } from 'drizzle-orm/node-postgres';
 925 |  3 | import { Pool, Client } from 'pg';
 926 |  4 | import { pgSchema } from 'drizzle-orm/pg-core';
 927 |  5 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
 928 |  6 | import { tenants } from './schema/shared';
 929 |  7 | import { usersColumns } from './schema/tenant';
 930 |  8 | import { env } from '../../env.mjs';
 931 |  9 | 
 932 | 10 | // Single shared pool for the entire database (all schemas)
 933 | 11 | const sharedPool = new Pool({ connectionString: env.DATABASE_URL });
 934 | 12 | export const sharedDb = drizzle(sharedPool);
 935 | 13 | 
 936 | 14 | // Function to get tenant-specific DB (dynamic schema qualification, same pool)
 937 | 15 | export async function getTenantDb(tenantId: string) {
 938 | 16 |   console.log(`[DB] Resolving tenant DB for ${tenantId}`);
 939 | 17 |   const tenant = await sharedDb.select().from(tenants).where(eq(tenants.tenantId, tenantId)).limit(1);
 940 | 18 |   if (!tenant.length) {
 941 | 19 |     console.error(`[DB] Tenant not found: ${tenantId}`);
 942 | 20 |     throw new Error('Tenant not found');
 943 | 21 |   }
 944 | 22 |   const schemaName = tenant[0].schemaName;
 945 | 23 | 
 946 | 24 |   const tenantSchema = pgSchema(schemaName);
 947 | 25 |   const users = tenantSchema.table('users', usersColumns);
 948 | 26 | 
 949 | 27 |   const tenantDb = drizzle(sharedPool, { schema: { users } });
 950 | 28 |   console.log(`[DB] Tenant DB initialized for schema: ${schemaName}`);
 951 | 29 |   return { db: tenantDb, schema: { users } };
 952 | 30 | }
 953 | 31 | 
 954 | 32 | // For raw queries (e.g., schema creation)
 955 | 33 | export async function executeRawQuery(query: string) {
 956 | 34 |   const client = new Client({ connectionString: env.DATABASE_URL });
 957 | 35 |   await client.connect();
 958 | 36 |   try {
 959 | 37 |     await client.query(query);
 960 | 38 |     console.log(`[DB] Executed raw query: ${query.substring(0, 50)}...`);
 961 | 39 |   } finally {
 962 | 40 |     await client.end();
 963 | 41 |   }
 964 | 42 | }
 965 | 43 | 
 966 | 44 | // Export types
 967 | 45 | export type TenantDb = Awaited<ReturnType<typeof getTenantDb>>;
 968 |

 974 |  2 | import { pgTable, serial, text, timestamp } from 'drizzle-orm/pg-core';
 975 |  3 | 
 976 |  4 | export const tenants = pgTable('tenants', {
 977 |  5 |   id: serial('id').primaryKey(),
 978 |  6 |   tenantId: text('tenant_id').notNull().unique(),
 979 |  7 |   schemaName: text('schema_name').notNull(),
 980 |  8 |   name: text('name').notNull(),
 981 |  9 |   createdAt: timestamp('created_at').defaultNow().notNull(),
 982 | 10 | });

 989 | 2 | import { serial, text } from 'drizzle-orm/pg-core';
 990 | 3 | 
 991 | 4 | export const usersColumns = {
 992 | 5 |   id: serial('id').primaryKey(),
 993 | 6 |   name: text('name').notNull(),
 994 | 7 |   email: text('email').notNull().unique(),
 995 | 8 |   password: text('password').notNull(),  // Hashed
 996 | 9 | };

1001 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
1002 |  1 | // lib/dto/tenant.ts
1003 |  2 | import { z } from 'zod';
1004 |  3 | 
1005 |  4 | export const TenantSignupDto = z.object({
1006 |  5 |   orgName: z.string().min(3, 'Org name must be at least 3 characters').max(50),
1007 |  6 |   tenantId: z.string().min(3, 'Tenant ID must be at least 3 characters').max(50).regex(/^[a-z0-9-]+$/, 'Tenant ID must be lowercase letters, numbers, or hyphens'),
1008 |  7 |   adminName: z.string().min(3, 'Admin name must be at least 3 characters').max(100),
1009 |  8 |   adminEmail: z.string().email('Invalid email'),
1010 |  9 |   adminPassword: z.string().min(8, 'Password must be at least 8 characters'),
1011 | 10 | });
1012 | 11 | 
1013 | 12 | export const LoginDto = z.object({
1014 | 13 |   email: z.string().email('Invalid email'),
1015 | 14 |   password: z.string().min(8, 'Password must be at least 8 characters'),
1016 | 15 | });
1017 | 16 | 
1018 | 17 | export type TenantSignupInput = z.infer<typeof TenantSignupDto>;
1019 | 18 | export type LoginInput = z.infer<typeof LoginDto>;

1025 |  1 | // lib/server/tenant.ts
1026 |  2 | import { sharedDb } from '@/lib/db';
1027 |  3 | import { tenants } from '@/lib/db/schema/shared';
1028 |  4 | import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
1029 |  5 | 
1030 |  6 | export async function validateTenant(tenantId: string) {
1031 |  7 |   console.log(`[Tenant] Validating tenant: ${tenantId}`);
1032 |  8 |   const tenant = await sharedDb.select().from(tenants).where(eq(tenants.tenantId, tenantId)).limit(1);
1033 |  9 |   if (!tenant.length) {
1034 | 10 |     console.error(`[Tenant] Invalid tenant: ${tenantId}`);
1035 | 11 |     throw new Error('Tenant not found');
1036 | 12 |   }
1037 | 13 |   return tenant[0];
1038 | 14 | }

1053 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
1054 | /middleware.ts:
1055 | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
1056 |  1 | // middleware.ts
1057 |  2 | import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
1058 |  3 | 
1059 |  4 | export async function middleware(request: NextRequest) {
1060 |  5 |   const host = request.headers.get('host') || '';
1061 |  6 |   const parts = host.split('.');
1062 |  7 |   const tenantId = parts.length > 2 ? parts[0] : null;  // e.g., tenant1.localhost:3000 → tenant1
1063 |  8 | 
1064 |  9 |   console.log(`[Middleware] Host: ${host}, Tenant ID: ${tenantId}`);
1065 | 10 | 
1066 | 11 |   // Public routes (no tenant needed) - added '/'
1067 | 12 |   const pathname = request.nextUrl.pathname;
1068 | 13 |   if (!tenantId && (pathname === '/' || pathname.startsWith('/signup') || pathname.startsWith('/login') || pathname.startsWith('/api/tenants') || pathname.startsWith('/api/auth'))) {
1069 | 14 |     return NextResponse.next();
1070 | 15 |   }
1071 | 16 | 
1072 | 17 |   console.log(`[Middleware] Tenant ID found: ${tenantId}`);
1073 | 18 |   if (!tenantId) {
1074 | 19 |     console.error('[Middleware] No tenant ID found');
1075 | 20 |     return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Tenant not found' }, { status: 404 });
1076 | 21 |   }
1077 | 22 | 
1078 | 23 |   // Set tenant context in headers (no validation here)
1079 | 24 |   const headers = new Headers(request.headers);
1080 | 25 |   headers.set('x-tenant-id', tenantId);
1081 | 26 |   console.log(`[Middleware] Setting x-tenant-id header: ${tenantId}`);
1082 | 27 |   console.log(`[Middleware] headers: ${JSON.stringify(Array.from(headers.entries()))}`);
1083 | 28 | 
1084 | 29 |   return NextResponse.next({ request: { headers } });
1085 | 30 | }
1086 | 31 | 
1087 | 32 | export const config = {
1088 | 33 |   matcher: ['/((?!_next/static|_next/image|favicon.ico).*)'],
1089 | 34 | };

/scripts/migrate-tenant.ts:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | // Create a new file: /scripts/migrate-tenant.ts
 2 | import { drizzle } from 'drizzle-orm/postgres-js';
 3 | import { migrate } from 'drizzle-orm/postgres-js/migrator';
 4 | import postgres from 'postgres';
 5 | import 'dotenv/config';
 6 | 
 7 | async function main() {
 8 |   const connectionString = process.env.TENANT_DATABASE_URL;
 9 | 
10 |   if (!connectionString) {
11 |     throw new Error('TENANT_DATABASE_URL environment variable is not set.');
12 |   }
13 | 
14 |   // Use postgres 'on-the-fly' with max 1 connection for migrations
15 |   const migrationClient = postgres(connectionString, { max: 1 });
16 |   const db = drizzle(migrationClient);
17 | 
18 |   console.log('Running migrations for tenant...');
19 | 
20 |   await migrate(db, { migrationsFolder: './drizzle/tenant' });
21 | 
22 |   console.log('Migrations completed successfully.');
23 | 
24 |   await migrationClient.end();
25 |   process.exit(0);
26 | }
27 | 
28 | main().catch((err) => {
29 |   console.error('Migration failed:', err);
30 |   process.exit(1);
31 | });
